  7. Scopus Q2 SJR 2025: 0.233 city evaluation

    A New System for Evaluating a Siberian City: Evaluation Methodology

    Antamoshkin O. A., Stupina A., Shagaeva O., Yamaletdinov S., Kuzmich R., Ruiga I.

    Civil Engineering and Architecture 9(5): 1318-1326, 2021 DOI: 10.13189/cea.2021.090505.

    2021 · Research Publications
